###########################
# Germany Decisions
###########################

political_actions = {

	GER_remove_schacht = {
		icon = GFX_decision_soldierly_discipline

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GER_remove_schacht_need_kaiser_approval_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
				}
				has_completed_focus = GER_prussia_privy_council
				custom_override_tooltip = {
					tooltip = GER_swr_balanced_or_dkp_tt
					OR = {
						GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
							has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_average
						}
						GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
							has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_low
						}
						GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
							has_trait = KR_leader_of_dvlp_min
						}
						NOT = {
							GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
								has_advisor_role = political_advisor
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_du_path = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = GER_SPD_rebellion
					GER_hofgeismar_circle = {
						is_political_advisor = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_left_spd_demands_4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
				}
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_override_tooltip = {
					tooltip = { localization_key = has_completed_decision DECISION = GER_red_general_new_state }
					has_country_flag = GER_red_general_new_state_flag
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_nullification_ongoing }
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_remove_schacht"
			country_event = germany_flavour_events.114
			set_country_flag = GER_schacht_removed
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	GER_war_preparedness_act = {
		icon = GFX_decision_soldierly_discipline

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			threat > 0.4
			has_completed_focus = GER_einkreisung
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_nationalise_rail
				has_completed_focus = GER_railway_nationalisation
				has_completed_focus = GER_military_railways
			}
			has_completed_focus = GER_industriewerke
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_infantry_development
				has_completed_focus = GER_artillery_development
			}
			check_variable = {
				tooltip = GER_five_industrial_decisions_tt
				GER_completed_industrial_decisions > 4
			}
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				second_weltkrieg_has_begun = yes
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_war_preparedness_act"
			increase_economic_mobilisation = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				increase_conscription = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_war_preparedness_act_tt
			set_country_flag = GER_war_preparedness_act_passed
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	GER_join_kaiser_wilhelm_society = {
		icon = generic_research

		allowed = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = FRA #always hostile
				tag = ENG
				tag = WCA
				tag = SRI
				tag = SWF
				tag = FOP
				tag = HND
				tag = RUS
				tag = JAP
				tag = FER
				tag = USA #can't join
				tag = ACC
				tag = NEE
				tag = RAJ
			}
			is_tag_in_china_area = no #can't join
		}

		targets = { GER }
		target_root_trigger = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
		target_trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
			NOT = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = german_research }
			FROM = {
				is_in_tech_sharing_group = german_research
				is_subject = no
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = AUS_intervened_in_weltkrieg
				has_country_flag = AUS_former_faction_member
			}
		}

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_join_kaiser_wilhelm_society"
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}
MIE_decisions_GER = {
	GER_invest_oststaat = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_agreement

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			country_exists = FROM
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 60
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					is_ai = no
					same_government_type_as_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove GER_invest_oststaat"
			FROM = {
				add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
				add_one_random_civilian_factory = yes
				add_ideas = GER_german_investment_oststaat_idea
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				country_event = germany_foreign_events_new.51
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = POL
					}
					effect_tooltip = {
						set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
						POL_add_german_influence = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}

crisis = {
	GER_black_monday_escalation = {
		icon = generic_inflation

		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_idea = GER_black_monday_10
		}

		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 10

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_black_monday_escalation"
			add_stability = -0.05
			GER_increase_black_monday = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = GER_black_monday_10 }
					country_event = germany_black_monday_events.4
				}
				else = {
					activate_mission = GER_black_monday_escalation
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}
GER_ruhrkampf_mechanics_category = {
	GER_ruhrkampf_escalation = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_ruhrkampf_begun }
		}

		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 25

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_ruhrkampf_escalation"
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_ruhrkampf_escalation_tt
			# events which kill your government if you are authdem and are not in this range
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_ruhrkampf_strength < 25 }
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_enabling_act
					}
					is_ai = no # AI can only die to the Reichstag mechanics.
					check_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats < 223 }
					check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats < 223 }
				}
				country_event = germany_schleicher_events.37
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_ruhrkampf_strength > 75 }
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_enabling_act
					}
					is_ai = no # AI can only die to the Reichstag mechanics.
					check_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats < 223 }
					check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats < 223 }
				}
				country_event = germany_schleicher_events.38
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GER_ruhrkampf_strength = 10 } # Measures strength. Need to be 25-75 at the end of each Ruhrkampf turn
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			activate_mission = GER_ruhrkampf_escalation
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	GER_ruhrkampf_occupy_east_rhineland = {
		icon = infiltrate_state

		allowed = { always = no }

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = 51
					size > 5
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 51 }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 14

		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_ruhrkampf_begun
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_ruhrkampf_occupy_east_rhineland"
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_manpower = -50
			subtract_from_variable = { # Measures strength. Need to be 25-75 at the end of each Ruhrkampf turn
				var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength
				value = 25
				tooltip = GER_ruhrkampf_reduced
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_ruhrkampf_occupy_east_rhineland"
			add_to_variable = { # Measures strength. Need to be 25-75 at the end of each Ruhrkampf turn
				var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength
				value = 15
				tooltip = GER_ruhrkampf_raised
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_ruhrkampf_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	GER_ruhrkampf_occupy_brunswick = {

		timeout_effect = {

				country_event = germany_schleicher_events.44
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no

foreign_politics = {
	GER_erode_cof_legitimacy = {
		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

		allowed = {
			NOT = { tag = FRA }
		}

		available = {
			FRA = { has_legitimacy > 20 }
		}

		visible = {
			FRA = { is_government_in_exile = yes }
			has_war_with = FRA
			is_subject = no
			is_in_array = { occupied_countries = FRA }
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 30
		cost = 25

		ai_will_do = { factor = 200 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_erode_cof_legitimacy"
			set_country_flag = GER_eroding_cof_leg
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove GER_erode_cof_legitimacy"
			clr_country_flag = GER_eroding_cof_leg
			if = {
				limit = { tag = NFA }
				FRA = {
					add_legitimacy = -25
					add_war_support = -0.15
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NFA
					NOT = { tag = GER }
				}
				FRA = {
					add_legitimacy = -15
					add_war_support = -0.10
				}
			}
			else = {
				FRA = {
					add_legitimacy = -10
					add_war_support = -0.05
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	GER_invite_nfa_to_france = {
		icon = generic_agreement

		allowed = { tag = GER }

		available = {
			FRA = { has_capitulated = yes }
		}

		visible = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			country_exists = FROM
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
			any_state_in = {
				strategic_region = 20 #Southern France
				is_controlled_by = GER
			}
			NOT = {
				FRA = {
					any_core_state = {
						count = 3
						is_controlled_by = NFA
					}
				}
			}
		}

		targets = { NFA }
		target_root_trigger = { has_war_with = FRA }
		target_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_eroding_cof_leg
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power > 50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FRA = { has_legitimacy < 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = ENG }
					ENG = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_invite_nfa_to_france"
			NFA = { country_event = capitulation_events.43 }
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	GER_deploy_troops_to_occupation_zones = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_manpower > 40000
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 5000 }
			has_equipment = { support_equipment > 1000 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = GER_deploy_troops_cost

		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			country_exists = FROM
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				GER_is_military_governorate = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = { political_power_gain = -0.1 }

		days_remove = 30
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_deploy_troops_to_occupation_zones"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_manpower = -40000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -5000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = -1000
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				add_manpower = 40000
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {

	GER_attack_syndicalists = {
		name = invade_country
		icon = generic_tank

		allowed = { original_tag = GER }

		available = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_british_tag = no
						NOT = { original_tag = IRE }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = FROM
					FROM = { any_home_area_neighbor_country = { is_ally_with = ROOT } }
					FROM = { capital_scope = { is_one_state_island = yes } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
			NOT = { has_guaranteed = FROM }
		}

		visible = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			OR = {
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_death_of_syndicalism
					FROM = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_death_of_syndicalism }
					FROM = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
					}
				}
				else = {
					FROM = { has_socialist_government = no }
				}
				is_faction_leader = no
				has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM
				has_guaranteed = FROM
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_government = social_democrat } }
					FROM = { is_in_faction = yes }
				}
			}
		}

		target_array = global.european_tags_array
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_destroy_europe_syndicalism
		}
		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			OR = {
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_death_of_syndicalism
					FROM = {
						has_government = social_democrat
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					country_has_any_active_threat = yes
					FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger = yes }
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision cancel GER_attack_syndicalists"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_attack_syndicalists"
			FROM = { incoming_war_notification_effect = yes }
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove GER_attack_syndicalists"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	GER_break_open_gibraltar = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			second_weltkrieg_can_start = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = yes }
				var:118.owner = {
					has_capitulated = no
					has_civil_war = no
					OR = {
						has_socialist_government = yes
						has_dictatorship_government = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				var:118.owner = {
					has_capitulated = no
					has_civil_war = no
					has_socialist_government = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = 118.owner }
			NOT = { has_guaranteed = 118.owner }
		}

		visible = {
			can_declare_war_on = 118.owner
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { can_declare_war_on = 118.owner }
				is_faction_leader = no
				second_weltkrieg_can_start = no
				var:118.owner = { has_civil_war = yes }
				var:118.owner = { has_capitulated = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { has_elected_government = yes }
					var:118.owner = {
						OR = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
							has_dictatorship_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					var:118.owner = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				}
				has_non_aggression_pact_with = 118.owner
				has_guaranteed = 118.owner
			}
		}

		cost = 15
		days_remove = 20
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_is_in_dangerous_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = SPA }
				has_game_rule = { rule = SPA_forpol option = SPA_FORPOL_GER }
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision cancel GER_break_open_gibraltar"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_break_open_gibraltar"
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove GER_break_open_gibraltar"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			add_state_claim = 118
			declare_war_on = {
				target = 118.owner
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

			build_railway = { # Improve rails in Saxony
				level = 1
				start_province = 6559
				target_province = 9570

			if = {
				limit = {

	GER_Infrastructure_Development = {

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GER_Ruhrkampf
					}
				}
			}
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
		}

		cost = 40
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		state_target = yes

			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

			factor = 20

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER_dont_spend_PP_industry = yes
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision remove GER_Infrastructure_Development"

				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}

				limit = {

GER_1936_election_category = {
	GER_SPD_consolidate_saxon_strongholds = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_propaganda_campaigns

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			check_variable = {
				tooltip = GER_two_available_actions
				GER_available_actions > 0
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_SPD_consolidate_saxon_strongholds"
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_available_actions = 1 }

			subtract_from_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats = 2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_DkP_seats = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_liberal_seats > 0 }
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_liberal_seats = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_SPD_seats
				value = 5
				tooltip = GER_SPD_gain
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_LVP_seats = 1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = {

GER_schleicher_mechanics_category = {
	GER_democratic_union_alignment_turn = { # SPD flanks from above
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_rally

		allowed = { always = no }

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		fixed_random_seed = no

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_democratic_union_alignment_turn"
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_democratic_union_seats > 222 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							AND = {
								is_ai = yes
								has_country_flag = GER_du_ai
							}
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_du_about_to_win_tt
					hidden_effect = { country_event = germany_schleicher_events.12 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_swr_about_to_win_tt
					hidden_effect = { country_event = germany_schleicher_events.13 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_du_frozen
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_democratic_union_alignment_frozen
			}
			else = {
				GER_democratic_union_alignment_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_seats > 222 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ai = no
							AND = {
								is_ai = yes
								has_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = germany_schleicher_events.13 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_country_flag = GER_du_ai
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = germany_schleicher_events.12 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_swr_frozen }
				}
				hidden_effect = { GER_swr_alignment_effect = yes }
			}
			GER_reset_reichstag_game = yes

			activate_mission = GER_democratic_union_alignment_turn
		}
	}
	GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_demand

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {

				tooltip = GER_is_free_faction

				tooltip = GER_enough_faction_targets

							state = 10

					OR = {

						state = 4

						state = 8
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_swr_ai
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						state = 10
						state = 9
						state = 12
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						state = 10
						state = 9
						state = 8
						state = 3
						state = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction"
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction_tt
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = GER_faction_targeted
				add_to_array = { GER.protected_factions_array = THIS }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GER_available_faction_targets = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				#activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = GER_Defend_Reichstag_Faction }
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

GER_conservative_revolution_mechanics_category = {
	GER_DVLP_emergency_conference = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse

		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 120

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_DVLP_emergency_conference"
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_DVLP_emergency_conference_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { GER_hugenberg_faction_rift < 50 } # Rift is under 50 percent
								set_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats_hug }
								divide_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats } # Find % of Hugenberg supporters in DVLP Reichstag
								check_variable = { DVLP_percents < 0.5 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { GER_hugenberg_faction_rift > 50 } # Rift is above 50 percent
								set_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats_hug }
								divide_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats } # Find % of Hugenberg supporters in DVLP Reichstag
								check_variable = { DVLP_percents < 0.25 } # If rift is high, Hugenberg is more likely to split
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = germany_swr_events.29
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_hugenberg_faction_rift < 50 } # Rift is under 50 percent
						set_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats_hug }
						divide_temp_variable = { DVLP_percents = GER_DVLP_seats } # Find % of Hugenberg supporters in DVLP Reichstag
						check_variable = { DVLP_percents > 0.5 }
					}
					country_event = germany_swr_events.31
				}
				else = {
					country_event = germany_swr_events.30
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
	GER_DVLP_hugenberg_alignment = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse

		allowed = { always = no }

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = { has_active_mission = GER_DVLP_emergency_conference }
		}

		is_good = no
		fixed_random_seed = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 20

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_DVLP_hugenberg_alignment"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_defended_from_hugenberg
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_hug = 3 }
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_DVLP_seats_hug max = var:GER_DVLP_seats min = 0 }
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_has = 3 }
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_DVLP_seats_has max = var:GER_DVLP_seats min = 0 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_strengthens_hugenberg_tt
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = GER_defended_from_hugenberg
				add_to_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_has = 2 }
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_DVLP_seats_hug max = var:GER_DVLP_seats min = 0 }
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_DVLP_seats_hug = 2 }
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_DVLP_seats_has max = var:GER_DVLP_seats min = 0 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_not_strengthens_hugenberg_tt
			}
			activate_mission = GER_DVLP_hugenberg_alignment
			hidden_effect = {
				# Random chance for someone to become a vulnerability
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = GER_schlange_vulnerability_fired
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							NOT = {
								has_character = GER_hans_schlange_schoningen
							}
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_schlange_vulnerability_fired
						activate_mission = GER_DVLP_schlange_schoningen_alignment
						activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_defend_schlange }
					}
					70 = {

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = GER_schmidt_vulnerability_fired
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_schmidt_vulnerability_fired
						activate_mission = GER_DVLP_schmidt_alignment
						activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_defend_schmidt }
					}
					60 = {

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = GER_levetzow_vulnerability_fired
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_levetzow_vulnerability_fired
						activate_mission = GER_DVLP_levetzow_alignment
						activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_defend_levetzow }
					}
					60 = {

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = GER_trotha_vulnerability_fired
						}
						set_country_flag = GER_trotha_vulnerability_fired
						activate_mission = GER_DVLP_trotha_alignment
						activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_hugenberg_defend_trotha }
					}
					80 = {

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}

					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty > 0 }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GER_Z_loyalty
					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Agrarian_loyalty > 0 }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GER_Agrarian_loyalty
					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_Agrarian_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Agrarian_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty > 0 }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GER_Polish_loyalty
					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_loyalty > 0 }
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty
					value = 5
					tooltip = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty_gain
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty max = 100 min = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_base
						add_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = 0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
					max = 0
					min = -1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor > -0.01 }
					}
					country_event = germany_spd_events.69
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_SPD_demand_civil_service_reform"
			add_political_power = -25
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_10

					}

					max = 0

				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
					check_variable = { GER_iron_front_organisation > 29 }
					NOT = {
						has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 20 }
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision timeout GER_brunswick_front_activity"
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
						add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
					max = 0
					min = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_ai = yes
							check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 } # AI cheat
						}
						AND = {
							is_ai = no
							check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = germany_spd_events.53
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
					has_country_flag = GER_papen_active_brunswick
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_papen_active_brunswick_tt
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_Z_loyalty
					value = 10
					tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
						is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
				}
			}
			activate_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_brunswick_front_activity"
			# add a hidden event which only fires this after 30 days or so
			add_to_variable = { GER_iron_front_organisation = -10 }

				add_political_power = -25

					check_variable = { GER_iron_front_organisation > 29 }
					NOT = {
						has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_base
						add_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = 0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
					max = 0
					min = -1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor > -0.01 }
					}
					country_event = germany_spd_events.69
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_iron_front_organisation = -10 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_iron_front_organisation_reduce_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_iron_front_brunswick_suppresses
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_iron_front_lacks_organisation
			}
			activate_mission = GER_iron_front_activity
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	GER_five_year_plan = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_decision

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			GER_wissell_moellendorff = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_wissell_decision_active
			}
			check_variable = {
				tooltip = GER_completed_wissell_plan_decisions_3_tt
				GER_completed_wissell_plan_decisions > 2
			}
		}

		cost = 30
		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 200
				has_country_flag = GER_pump_priming_flag
				has_country_flag = GER_association_industry_flag
				has_country_flag = GER_association_iron_steel_industrialists_flag
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot][GetLogFrom]: Decision complete GER_five_year_plan"
			set_country_flag = GER_five_year_plan_flag
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { FROM.wissell_plan_array = THIS }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Central_Economic_Management_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Central_Economic_Management }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_country_flag = GER_pump_priming_flag
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_country_flag = GER_association_industry_flag
						}
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							has_country_flag = GER_association_iron_steel_industrialists_flag
						}
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = steel
						amount = 8
					}
				}
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}
}
GER_anti_sedition_laws_category = {
	GER_anti_sedition_karl_korsch = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_arrest

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 20
		days_remove = 30

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_idea = civilian_economy
					has_idea = volunteer_only
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision remove GER_anti_sedition_karl_korsch"
			add_war_support = 0.02
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_to_variable = { GER_anti_sedition_decisions_complete = 1 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = -0.01
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_anti_sedition_decisions_complete > 6 }
				}
				country_event = germany_events.53
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_army_support

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 30

		available = {
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = { localization_key = has_completed_decision DECISION = GER_red_general_new_state }
				has_country_flag = GER_red_general_new_state_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SCHLEICHER_AUTDEM }
				OR = {
					has_idea = GER_new_state_5
					AND = {
						has_idea = GER_new_state_4
						has_country_flag = GER_anti_democratic_civil_service_ongoing
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_red_general_intimidate_reichstag"
			if = {
				limit = {
					custom_override_tooltip = {
						tooltip = { localization_key = has_completed_decision DECISION = GER_red_general_new_state }
						has_country_flag = GER_red_general_new_state_flag
					}
				}
				GER_increase_new_state = yes
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_new_state_1
					add_idea = GER_new_state_2
				}
				# only exists for tooltip
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_army_support

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 40
		days_remove = 200
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = -0.1
			production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.05
			political_power_factor = -0.15
		}

		available = {
			check_variable = {
				tooltip = GER_schleicher_left_only
				GER_schleicher_ideology > 66
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Decision complete GER_red_general_seize_industries"
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = yes }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = yes }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					free_building_slots = { building = industrial_complex size > 0 include_locked = yes }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schleicher_move_left
			add_to_variable = { GER_schleicher_ideology = 20 }
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_schleicher_ideology max = 100 min = 0 }
